Description Enhances Empress's Blessing effects.
Level 1 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 1
6 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 6

Master Level 6
Description Enhances Empress's Blessing effects.
Level 1 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 1

4 Increase Empress's Blessing max level by 4

Active Hero's Echo
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Elemental Slash
Master Level 1
Description Attack enemies in front of you with pure, primal energy.
Level 1 MP Cost: 0, Damage: 130%, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 3


Active Imperial Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to the Empress using Shinsoo's power.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, return to Ereve immediately.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Passive Elemental Harmony
Master Level 1
Description Use the harmony of nature to build affinity for an element of your choosing.
Level 1 Strength increases 1 for every 2 levels the character gains


Passive Elemental Expert
Master Level 1
Description Become an expert of the elements to increase Attack Power and Magic ATT.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +10%


Passive Elemental Shift
Master Level 1
Description Jump in any direction except down by pressing a direction key and jump in midair.
Level 1 MP Cost: 4, jumps further in the appropriate direction
Show/hide all levels
Passive Cygnus Blessing (Pirate)
Master Level 10
Description Blessings from an awakened Empress Cygnus protect you from harm.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 5 times, once for each unique Cygnus Knights job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +7, Abnormal Status Resistance: +1, All Elemental Resistance: +1%
10 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +25, Abnormal Status Resistance: +15, All Elemental Resistance: +15%

Active Flash
Master Level 15
Description Charges into enemies to deal damage. Charges forward if there are no enemies. Can be linked with all skills excluding Thunder and itself. The casting action can be canceled by linking with Tidal Crash in the air.
Level 1 MP Cost: 16, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 254%, Number of Attacks: 1
When no enemies are around, you'll be teleported forward 300.
15 MP Cost: 9, Max Enemies Hit: 4, Damage: 310%, Number of Attacks: 1
When no enemies are around, you'll be teleported forward 300.

Active Lightning Elemental
Master Level 10
Description Summons a blue-white lightning element to gain its power.
Can be toggled On/Off with the skill key.
Level 1 Chance to create 1 Lightning Charge: 1%, Buff Duration: 30 sec
Same chance to create 2 Lightning Charge when linking skill
Max Lightning Charge Stacks: 2
Ignore Enemy Defense: 1% per Lightning Charge
Consuming Lightning Charge temporarily applies adjusted buff for 10 sec that increases the same amount of stats as those increased by the consumed Lightning Charge
While adjusted buff is active, adjusted buff stacks decrease when Lightning Charge is obtained
All stats increased by Lightning Charge and adjusted buff are additive.
10 Chance to create 1 Lightning Charge: 10%, Buff Duration: 30 sec
Same chance to create 2 Lightning Charge when linking skill
Max Lightning Charge Stacks: 2
Ignore Enemy Defense: 5% per Lightning Charge
Consuming Lightning Charge temporarily applies adjusted buff for 10 sec that increases the same amount of stats as those increased by the consumed Lightning Charge
While adjusted buff is active, adjusted buff stacks decrease when Lightning Charge is obtained
All stats increased by Lightning Charge and adjusted buff are additive.

Active Tidal Crash
Master Level 20
Description Surge forward like ocean waves to sweep up enemies in range. (Some monsters can resist the sweep effect).
Can be canceled by holding the down key while surging forward. Can be linked with all skills, excluding Thunder and itself. The wave activates by canceling the skill that was used first. Some skills can link faster with Tidal Crash than other skills. Tidal Crash doesn't generate Lightning Charge.
With Action Customization enabled, you can cancel the skill by pressing its key again, without use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 198%, Number of Attacks: 2 while moving forward
20 MP Cost: 20, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 255%, Number of Attacks: 2 while moving forward

Passive Sea Wave
Master Level 15
Description [Link Mastery Skill]
Linking the skill imbues it with the power of lightning and creates a wave that flows towards the enemy. Sea Wave flows in the direction Thunder Breaker is facing when created, searching for the direction with more enemies to attack within a fixed range.
Attacks enemies it runs into while flowing, and is unaffected by attack reflection.
Right-click to lock Sea Wave activation.
Level 1 MP Cost: 22, created when linking skill and not under cooldown
Flows in a fixed direction, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 162%, Number of Attacks: 4
Disappears when moving a distance of 2700 or the number of enemies attacked is 24
Max Attack on Single Enemy: 1
Cooldown: 12 sec
15 MP Cost: 50, created when linking skill and not under cooldown
Flows in a fixed direction, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 190%, Number of Attacks: 4
Disappears when moving a distance of 2700 or the number of enemies attacked is 24
Max Attack on Single Enemy: 1
Cooldown: 12 sec

Active Gale
Master Level 20
Description [Link Mastery Skill]
Unleashes the power gained from using link skills at once. Can be linked with all skills excluding Thunder and itself. The casting action can be canceled by linking with Tidal Crash in the air.
Level 20 required to learn Typhoon.
Level 1 MP Cost: 45, can be used when Lightning Charge stack is 3
Uses all Lightning Charge stacks, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 324%, Number of Attacks: 3. When used at max Lightning Charge stacks, Damage: +21% points
Damage: +2% per Lightning Charge used, Buff Duration: 3 sec
However, this skill doesn't generate Lightning Charges.
Cooldown: 30 sec
20 MP Cost: 65, can be used when Lightning Charge stack is 3
Uses all Lightning Charge stacks, Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 381%, Number of Attacks: 3. When used at max Lightning Charge stacks, Damage: +40% points
Damage: +2% per Lightning Charge used, Buff Duration: 60 sec
However, this skill doesn't generate Lightning Charges.
Cooldown: 20 sec

Passive Typhoon
Master Level 30
Description [Link Mastery Skill]
Enhances Gale to maximize energy collection from using linked skills, transforming it into a devastating typhoon. Can be linked with all skills, excluding Thunder and itself. Can link faster with Tidal Crash. The casting action can be canceled by linking with Tidal Crash in the air.
Required Skill: Gale Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 34, can be used when Lightning Charge stack is 2
Uses all Lightning Charge stacks, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 233%, Number of Attacks: 5. When used at max Lightning Charge stacks, Damage: +71% points

Master Level 1

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF

Cooldown: 60 sec

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 41
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.

Active Empress Cygnus's Blessing
Master Level 25
Description The blessing of Cygnus increases damage and restores HP over time. This skill can be enhanced after Lv. 245. Affected by effects which reduce cooldown.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Duration: 45 sec, Damage +1%
Periodically restores 4% HP and increases your damage by 4%.
This damage bonus is additive and maxes out at 90%
Cooldown: 120 sec.
25 MP Cost: 500, Duration: 45 sec, Damage +25%
Periodically restores 4% HP and increases your damage by 5%.
This damage bonus is additive and maxes out at 90%
Cooldown: 120 sec.
30 MP Cost: 500, Duration: 45 sec, Damage +30%
Periodically restores 4% HP and increases your damage by 6%.
This damage bonus is additive and maxes out at 90%
Cooldown: 120 sec.

Active Loaded Dice
Master Level 25
Description The next time you use Roll of the Dice, you get to throw an extra die and choose your desired number (via the number keys). Jobs without Roll of the Dice will be allowed to use the Roll of the Dice skill and choose their desired number.
Level 1 HP Cost: 1000, select your desired die roll.
If a job that has Double Down gets the same number on 2 dice, the chance for the last die to have the same number is decreased by 50%.
Cooldown: 10 Sec.
[Passive Effect: Attack Power: +11]
25 HP Cost: 1000, select your desired die roll.
If a job that has Double Down gets the same number on 2 dice, the chance for the last die to have the same number is decreased by 50%.
Cooldown: 10 Sec.

Master Level 25
Description Puts your weapon into overdrive to unleash more attack power. Afterwards, your weapon will be less effective for a short while and cannot be unequipped until it's back to normal.

Active Lightning Cascade
Master Level 25
Description Call upon the full power of the storm to annihilate your enemies with a chain of lightning. Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 Active Effect: MP Cost: 1000. Grants Final Damage +12% for 37 sec. Initial Damage: 360%, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Number of Attacks: 6. Send forth a lightning bolt.
The damage it deals decreases with each enemy it attacks, and it can hit up to 4 nearby enemies in a row.
When only one bolt triggers, it becomes a more powerful version, dealing 416% damage 7 times.
Lightning Spawn Cooldown: 3 sec.
Passive Effect: when you attack when the active effect of Lightning Cascade isn't active, 1 lightning bolt activates if there are normal enemies nearby. Cooldown:6 sec. Active and Passive Effects cannot trigger simultaneously.
Skill Cooldown: 120 sec.
25 Active Effect: MP Cost: 1000. Grants Final Damage +24% for 49 sec. Initial Damage: 600%, Max Enemies Hit: 5, Number of Attacks: 6. Send forth a lightning bolt.

Passive Effect: when you attack when the active effect of Lightning Cascade isn't active, 1 lightning bolt activates if there are normal enemies nearby. Cooldown:6 sec. Active and Passive Effects cannot trigger simultaneously.

Active Lightning God Spear Strike
Master Level 25
Description [Link Mastery Skill]
The spear of the Thunder God appears and attacks nearby enemies. Can be linked with all skills except for itself, and is unaffected by attack reflection.
Turn on Auto Mode to automatically activate Lightning God Spear Strike whenever it is not on cooldown.
Auto Mode On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 500
A divine trident is obtained after 8 linked attacks land successfully.
Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 156%, Number of Attacks: 6
Afterwards, activates Lightning at set intervals 4 times, which hits up to 8 enemies for 208% damage 7 times.
Cooldown: 7 sec

Active Thunder Wall Sea Wave
Master Level 30
Description Pummels foes with a fist of lightning that splits the seas. With the power of the storm in your hands, even the heavens shall tremble.
When used, Lightning Elemental's Lightning Charge and Link Mastery are applied with max stacks. All Thunder Wall Sea Wave attacks are treated as linked attacks.

Lv. 10: Ignore Defense +20%
Lv. 20: Boss Damage +20%
Lv. 30: Ignore Defense +30% and Boss Damage +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1200, Invincible during casting
Shock Wave that attacks up to 15 enemies with 723% damage 5 times is triggered 32 times,
then Shock Wave that attacks with 703% damage 7 times is triggered 62 times
Cooldown: 360 sec
30 MP Cost: 1200, Invincible during casting
Shock Wave that attacks up to 15 enemies with 1390% damage 5 times is triggered 32 times,
then Shock Wave that attacks with 1370% damage 7 times is triggered 62 times
Cooldown: 360 sec

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Active HEXA Annihilate
Master Level 30
Description Summon a massive charge of electricity to blast enemies in front of you. Enemies hit by HEXA Annihilate are left with Lightning Brand.
HEXA Annihilate can be linked with all skills, excluding Lightning Charge and itself. Can link faster with Tidal Crash. The casting action can't be canceled by linking with Tidal Crash in the air.

Create a Lightning Brand on enemies hit that lasts 90 sec.

Active Thunder Bolt
Master Level 30
Description Attack an enemy branded by the Lightning Brand, dropping lightning on them. Lightning Spear Multistrike's linked attack and Thunder Wall Sea Wave can't create a brand on enemies.
By combining the power of the brand and lightning, a massive thunderbolt falls on a branded enemy when they are attacked with linked skills (excluding Sea Wave, Lightning Spear Multistrike's linked attack, and Thunder Wall Sea Wave). Lightning Strike and the thunderbolt are unaffected by attack reflection.
Required Skill: Annihilate Lv.30
Level 1 When attacking Lightning Brand marked enemies with a direct attack skill (excluding HEXA Annihilate and Tidal Crash), Lightning Strike hits the enemy. Damage: 206%, Number of Attacks: 3
Create a massive thunderbolt instead when using linked skills (excluding Sea Wave, Lightning Spear Multistrike's linked attack, and Thunder Wall Sea Wave). Damage: 166%, Number of Attacks: 5
Boss Damage: +40%, Ignore Defense: +20%
30 When attacking Lightning Brand marked enemies with a direct attack skill (excluding HEXA Annihilate and Tidal Crash), Lightning Strike hits the enemy. Damage: 380%, Number of Attacks: 3
Create a massive thunderbolt instead when using linked skills (excluding Sea Wave, Lightning Spear Multistrike's linked attack, and Thunder Wall Sea Wave). Damage: 340%, Number of Attacks: 5
Boss Damage: +40%, Ignore Defense: +20%

Active HEXA Thunderbolt
Master Level 30
Description Call down a destructive bolt of electricity in front of you. Can be linked with all skills, excluding Thunder and itself. Can link faster with Tidal Crash.
Periodically uses Thunder Slash instead, which calls down a thunderclap that sweeps across a wide area.
With Action Customization enabled, Thunder Slash only activates when using the skill while holding Up key.
Permanently enhances Lightning Strike's massive thunderbolt.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization On/Off
Required Skill: Thunderbolt Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 77, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 341%, Number of Attacks: 5
Thunder Slash: MP Cost: 80, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 371%, Number of Attacks: 5
Creates a Sea Wave in the direction that the character is facing. Sea Waves created by Thunder Slash are unaffected by cooldowns.
Cooldown: 6 sec
[Passive Effect: Lightning Strike's Massive Thunderbolt Damage: +99%p]
30 MP Cost: 84, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 515%, Number of Attacks: 5
Thunder Slash: MP Cost: 90, Max Enemies Hit: 12, Damage: 545%, Number of Attacks: 5
Creates a Sea Wave in the direction that the character is facing. Sea Waves created by Thunder Slash are unaffected by cooldowns.
Cooldown: 6 sec
[Passive Effect: Lightning Strike's Massive Thunderbolt Damage: +360%p]

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
